tamb\u00e9m trouxe estresse para o IBOVESPA, que cedeu 5.38% na semana.\nO caf\u00e9, tanto em Nova Iorque como em Londres, n\u00e3o conseguiu se desvencilhar da realiza\u00e7\u00e3o das commodities e devolveu ganhos recentes, tendo o primeiro encerrado nas m\u00ednimas da semana.\nUm dos principais fatores negativos para o ar\u00e1bica foi o enfraquecimento acentuado do spread dezembro/mar\u00e7o com uma queda de 25% no final da sess\u00e3o de segunda-feira e mantendo a fraqueza na ter\u00e7a-feira. Tecnicamente indica falta de interesse de recebedor, muito embora o assunto \u00e9 mais denso pois envolve localiza\u00e7\u00e3o do invent\u00e1rio, qualidade, etc.\nOs fundos vendo uma curva mais inclinada da estrutura (spreads) pouco se interessam em comprar o mercado, pelo contr\u00e1rio, pois \u00e9 uma forte indica\u00e7\u00e3o de venda e, portanto, o terminal durante o restante dos dias n\u00e3o encontrou for\u00e7a para sustentar.\nA influ\u00eancia macroecon\u00f4mica \u00e9 predominante no fim das contas, pois como mencionado dois par\u00e1grafos acima a press\u00e3o de venda foi generalizada para as commodities e para o caf\u00e9 na ICE tem o agravante dos participantes estarem ativos rolando suas posi\u00e7\u00f5es antes do per\u00edodo de entrega de dezembro.\nA consolida\u00e7\u00e3o das cota\u00e7\u00f5es e o posicionamento dos comitentes d\u00e1 a impress\u00e3o do mercado estar pr\u00f3ximo do \u201cpre\u00e7o-justo\u201d, provavelmente desenhando um intervalo de negocia\u00e7\u00e3o entre US$ 110.00 e US$ 130 centavos por libra peso at\u00e9 alguma novidade aparecer.\nNovidades podem vir de um fortalecimento do Real \u2013 ou uma enxurrada de vendas caso Bolsonaro e equipe n\u00e3o consigam se movimentar para aprovar as reformas necess\u00e1rias em 2019 \u2013 ou mesmo sobre o clima, dado alguns institutos estarem falando de uma maior chance de ano com El Nino.\nO Departamento de Agricultura dos Estados Unidos, USDA em ingl\u00eas, revisou sua estimativa para a safra corrente brasileira para 63.4 milh\u00f5es de sacas, pr\u00f3ximo dos 63.5 milh\u00f5es que tenho usado para exercitar o S&D mundial. Do total, 46.9 milh\u00f5es de sacas s\u00e3o de ar\u00e1bica e 16.5 milh\u00f5es de sacas s\u00e3o conilon, acima das 44.5 e 15.7 milh\u00f5es de sacas, respectivamente estimavas no relat\u00f3rio de maio.\nTecnicamente a quebra dos 113.90 (base o contrato de mar\u00e7o) deve animar os especuladores a voltarem a vender o terminal, enquanto uma movimenta\u00e7\u00e3o acima de 121.70 cts pode animar novamente os altistas.\nN\u00e3o haver\u00e1 coment\u00e1rio de caf\u00e9 nas duas pr\u00f3ximas semanas, volto a escrever no final de semana do dia 30 de novembro.\nBons feriados a todos (o Thanksgiving \u2013 A\u00e7\u00e3o de Gra\u00e7as - \u00e9 um dos principais nos Estados Unidos).\nRodrigo Costa*\n*Rodrigo Corr\u00eaa da Costa escreve este relat\u00f3rio sobre caf\u00e9 semanalmente como colaborador da Archer Consulting O RELAT\u00d3RIO DESTA SEMANA EST\u00c1 SENDO DISTRIBU\u00cdDO PARA 4451 PESSOAS Este relat\u00f3rio foi preparado pela Archer Consulting - Assessoria em Mercados de Futuros, Op\u00e7\u00f5es e Derivativos Ltda para uso exclusivo do destinat\u00e1rio, podendo, no entanto, ser reproduzido ou distribu\u00eddo por este a qualquer pessoa desde que citada a fonte. Therefore, presenting a full history to a doctor to account for the context of the illness is essential.Reducing your risk of infection Hantavirus is primarily found in rural areas, spread through the urine and droppings of deer mice, although other rodents capable of spreading it also include the white-footed mouse and the hispid cotton rat.Chiu advises those who have a history of exposure, have recently been camping or spent time in an enclosed space such as a summer cabin, or have a history of going hiking in the woods to keep a watchful eye on potential symptoms that may occur.Rural and outdoor exposures can put you at potential risk of hantavirus infection.Samuel T. Smallidge, a wdlife specialist at New Mexico State University, further suggests a few simple steps everyone can take to stay safe.\u201cIf you are entering into a confined space, for example a shed or an outbuilding or a barn, the recommendation is to open all doors and windows and walk away and leave it for at least 30 minutes,\u201d he told Healthline. \u201cWhat that allows to happen is the finest particulate matter in that space that\u2019s closed up will have an opunity to be disturbed by the breeze.\n",

The recent death of a 9-year-old boy in New Mexico has raised concerns about hantavirus \u2014 a rare but frequently deadly infection spread through secretions of deer mice. Fernando Hernandez of Bloomfield, New Mexico, succumbed to the illness at the Cincinnati Children\u2019s Hospital nine months after his initial diagnosis. Symptoms of hantavirus \u2014 or more specifically Sin Nombre virus, the strain of hantavirus found in the United States \u2014 can often appear benign at onset and are often described as flu-like. Involving muscle aches, fever, and fatigue, the disease can rapidly progress to dangerous infection of the lungs called hantavirus pulmonary syndrome (HPS). The first stages of HPS typically appear as shortness of breath and cough and typically occur within two weeks of infection but can appear as late as six weeks. In later stages, the lungs actually begin to fill with fluid, a condition known as pulmonary edema, leading to severe breathing difficulties and increased stress on the cardiovascular system.\u201cWhat that really is is a viral pneumonia that can essentially expand to involve basically the rest of the body. Patients can become critically ill very quickly if they become infected with hantavirus,\u201d Dr. Charles Chiu, an infectious disease specialist at University of California, San Francisco, told Healthline. \u201cIt can actually progress to respiratory failure where you would have to be supported by a mechanical ventilator.\u201d Such was the case of Fernando Hernandez.\n",
